        }

          width: 100%;

Email display settings

<h2>Email display settings</h2>



        

There is a 

setting

<a href="/hosting/settings">setting</a>

 to control how
        your email address appears on comments and issues that you post.

<p>There is a <a href="/hosting/settings">setting</a> to control how
        your email address appears on comments and issues that you post.</p>



        

Project members will always see your full email address.  By
        default, other users who visit the site will see an
        abbreviated version of your email address.

<p>Project members will always see your full email address.  By
        default, other users who visit the site will see an
        abbreviated version of your email address.</p>



        

If you do not wish your email address to be shared, there
        are other ways to 

get
        involved

<a href="http://www.chromium.org/getting-involved">get
        involved</a>

 in the community.  To report a problem when using
        the Chrome browser, you may use the "Report an issue..."  item
        on the "Help" menu.

<p>If you do not wish your email address to be shared, there
        are other ways to <a href="http://www.chromium.org/getting-involved">get
        involved</a> in the community.  To report a problem when using
        the Chrome browser, you may use the "Report an issue..."  item
        on the "Help" menu.</p>

This site hosts public issues in public projects

<h2>This site hosts public issues in public projects</h2>



        

Unlike our internal issue tracker, this site makes most
        issues public, unless the issue is labeled with a Restrict-View-*
        label, such as Restrict-View-Google.

<p>Unlike our internal issue tracker, this site makes most
        issues public, unless the issue is labeled with a Restrict-View-*
        label, such as Restrict-View-Google.</p>



        

Components are not used for permissions.  And, regardless of
        restriction labels, the issue reporter, owner,
        and Cc'd users may always view the issue.

<p>Components are not used for permissions.  And, regardless of
        restriction labels, the issue reporter, owner,
        and Cc'd users may always view the issue.</p>

        label, such as Restrict-View-Google.</p>

        restriction labels, the issue reporter, owner,
        and Cc'd users may always view the issue.</p>

VULNERABILITY DETAILS



<b class="line"><!---->VULNERABILITY DETAILS<!----></b>



<br>





In zlib a potential buffer overflow was fixed recently. See: 



<span class="line"><!---->In zlib a potential buffer overflow was fixed recently. See: <!----></span>





https://github.com/madler/zlib/commit/eff308af425b67093bab25f80f1ae950166bece1



<a class="undefined" target="_blank" href="https://github.com/madler/zlib/commit/eff308af425b67093bab25f80f1ae950166bece1"><!---->https://github.com/madler/zlib/commit/eff308af425b67093bab25f80f1ae950166bece1<!----></a>



<br>





The fix introduced a null pointer deref, which was fixed as well. See: 



<span class="line"><!---->The fix introduced a null pointer deref, which was fixed as well. See: <!----></span>





https://github.com/madler/zlib/commit/1eb7682f845ac9e9bf9ae35bbfb3bad5dacbd91d



<a class="undefined" target="_blank" href="https://github.com/madler/zlib/commit/1eb7682f845ac9e9bf9ae35bbfb3bad5dacbd91d"><!---->https://github.com/madler/zlib/commit/1eb7682f845ac9e9bf9ae35bbfb3bad5dacbd91d<!----></a>



<br>



<br>





The fix is in zlib develop branch at this point in time, not reached zlib master yet.



<span class="line"><!---->The fix is in zlib develop branch at this point in time, not reached zlib master yet.<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





VERSION



<b class="line"><!---->VERSION<!----></b>



<br>





The corrections are not in Chromium master yet - somehow expectable. If exploitable in Chromium as well, could you please update zlib accordingly, probably once this reached a stable version in zlib?



<span class="line"><!---->The corrections are not in Chromium master yet - somehow expectable. If exploitable in Chromium as well, could you please update zlib accordingly, probably once this reached a stable version in zlib?<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





CREDIT INFORMATION



<b class="line"><!---->CREDIT INFORMATION<!----></b>



<br>





Originally found by Evgeny Legerov of @intevydis, see 



<span class="line"><!---->Originally found by Evgeny Legerov of @intevydis, see <!----></span>





https://github.com/ivd38/zlib_overflow



<a class="undefined" target="_blank" href="https://github.com/ivd38/zlib_overflow"><!---->https://github.com/ivd38/zlib_overflow<!----></a>





.



<span class="line"><!---->.<!----></span>





 I (Richard Lorenz from SAP) just stumbled across this one in our open source scans, because we integrated Chromium Embedded Framework within SAP Business Client.



<span class="line"><!----> I (Richard Lorenz from SAP) just stumbled across this one in our open source scans, because we integrated Chromium Embedded Framework within SAP Business Client.<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





Best regards,



<span class="line"><!---->Best regards,<!----></span>



<br>





Richard



<span class="line"><!---->Richard<!----></span>

 - Change version number on develop branch to 1.2.12.1.



<span class="line"><!----> - Change version number on develop branch to 1.2.12.1.<!----></span>



<br>





 - Fix odd error in Visual C compiler preventing automatic promotion.



<span class="line"><!----> - Fix odd error in Visual C compiler preventing automatic promotion.<!----></span>



<br>





 - Fix inflateBack to detect invalid input with distances too far.



<span class="line"><!----> - Fix inflateBack to detect invalid input with distances too far.<!----></span>



<br>





 - Have infback() deliver all of the available output up to any error.



<span class="line"><!----> - Have infback() deliver all of the available output up to any error.<!----></span>



<br>





 - Fix a bug when getting a gzip header extra field with inflate().



<span class="line"><!----> - Fix a bug when getting a gzip header extra field with inflate().<!----></span>



<br>





 - Fix extra field processing bug that dereferences NULL state->head.



<span class="line"><!----> - Fix extra field processing bug that dereferences NULL state-&gt;head.<!----></span>



<br>





 - Fix some typos.



<span class="line"><!----> - Fix some typos.<!----></span>

*** Boilerplate reminders! ***



<span class="line"><!---->*** Boilerplate reminders! ***<!----></span>



<br>





Please do NOT publicly disclose details until a fix has been released to all our users. Early public disclosure may cancel the provisional reward. Also, please be considerate about disclosure when the bug affects a core library that may be used by other products. Please do NOT share this information with third parties who are not directly involved in fixing the bug. Doing so may cancel the provisional reward. Please be honest if you have already disclosed anything publicly or to third parties. Lastly, we understand that some of you are not interested in money. We offer the option to donate your reward to an eligible charity. If you prefer this option, let us know and we will also match your donation - subject to our discretion. Any rewards that are unclaimed after 12 months will be donated to a charity of our choosing.



<span class="line"><!---->Please do NOT publicly disclose details until a fix has been released to all our users. Early public disclosure may cancel the provisional reward.  - Fix some typos.



<span class="line"><!----> - Fix some typos.<!----></span>
